Record of the Continued Trial of the China Merchants' Bureau Embezzlement Case

Police Officer Li Guojie Escorted to Court

Li Confesses That Chen Took Away 700,000

Dou Yaoting Testifies That He Does Not Know the Details

Li Guojie, the general manager of the China Merchants' Bureau, was accused of borrowing foreign debt, embezzling, breaching trust, and harming the interests of the bureau, as well as bribing Chen Fumu, the supervisor, with 700,000 taels. The Shanghai District Court sentenced him to three years in prison. He appealed, and the High Court, led by Lin Zhezhang, presiding judge of the Criminal Division One, judges Fang Wen and Si Wen, prosecutor Chen Guifen, and clerks Qian Zemin and Li Wang, came to Shanghai and temporarily used the First Tribunal of the Shanghai District Court for the trial. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM was the time for the continuation of the trial. Li Guojie still retained defense lawyers Zhang Yipeng, Sha Xunyi, and Jiang Yiping, while Liu Hongsheng, the current general manager of the China Merchants' Bureau, retained lawyer Wang Youling to represent him due to the 700,000 yuan. Wang was not present, and lawyer Liu Zhen acted as a substitute. After the judge opened the court, police chief Chen Junfang, police officers Chen Xihui and Zhu Wenqing, and others escorted Li to the court from the Shanghai Hospital, helping him up to the courtroom. The judge still allowed Li to sit and give his testimony. The clerk first read aloud the previous testimony, which was the same, and Li was ordered to sign it. Then, the judge (asked) Li Guojie, what do you mean by this letter from the Minister of Transportation? (Answer) I am reporting that the procedures for these 700,000 taels are incomplete, and I have unavoidable hardships. (Question) What hardships? (Answer) After Chen Fumu took the 700,000 taels, he did not hand them over during the handover, and he did not give them to the relief office. I was very anxious. (Question) When the money was handed over that day, Dou Yaoting brought the money, and Huang Jusu brought the contract. Did you handle most of it? (Answer) Because the supervisor said that when doing business with foreigners, it is necessary to pay an advance, so after negotiating with the business company two weeks ago, the supervisor said that this payment must be kept by him, otherwise, he was afraid that the China Merchants' Bureau would be too poor and it would be used for other purposes. (Question) Where is Wang Yunzhang now? (Answer) I don't know. (Question) Where did Huang Jusu go? (Answer) I don't know. Wang Yunzhang was my English secretary. (Question) Dou Yaoting, you are 45 years old, from Ningbo, and live at 70 Sichuan Road. The China Business Company does real estate business. (Question) Today you are here as a witness, you must tell the truth. After he signed an affidavit, he was again (asked) Who is your manager? (Answer) Sadeli (Question) Was the 700,000 advance paid to you? (Answer) Yes. (Question) What kind of money was it? (Answer) It was what the head clerk said was paid to the China Merchants' Bureau. (Question) What did he say at the time? (Answer) I don't know, but I sent the money and took the receipt back. (Question) Did he explain it to you? (Answer) He said that the deposit was sent. (Question) Did you talk about it with the manager before? (Answer) This was probably known to the old manager (old Sadeli), we didn't know. (Question) What was the 700,000? (Answer) Presented bank notes, a total of fourteen, eleven of which were silver. (Question) I want to ask you where you handed the money over. (Answer) The office under the China Merchants' Bureau. (Question) Who did you hand it over to? (Answer) To Mr. Li. (Question) How did you hand it to him? (Answer) As soon as I went, he knew, and after taking the payment, he gave me a receipt, which was in foreign characters and had a seal. I saw that it was correct, so I left. He told me to give me a package, saying that the contract had been taken back. I didn't look at the contents either. (Question) If it wasn't a contract, wouldn't you have looked at it? (Answer) Because the old manager didn't tell me, so after giving me a package, I didn't look into it. (Question) Did anyone else come? (Answer) Many people came and went. (Question) Do you know Huang Jusu? (Answer) There is such a person, whom I met three years ago when he came to the company for other business. I don't know if it's the same person. (Question) Did Huang Jusu meet you when you paid the money that day? (Answer) I didn't pay attention. (Question) Was Wang Yunzhang there? (Answer) This is Mr. Li's English secretary, I know him, but I didn't see him that day. I left in a hurry. (Question) After Li Guojie received the 700,000, who did he give it to? (Answer) I didn't see that. (Question) What time was it that day? (Answer) Four o'clock in the afternoon on September 13th. (Question) What is the nature of Sassoon & Co.? (Answer) They specialize in lending money and don't do retail business. They have another Mercari Bank. (Question) Did Sadeli come? (Answer) He didn't come. At this point, (asked again) Li Guojie, what is the interest rate on the 700,000 taels? (Answer) It is calculated from the date of receipt. (Question) Has the contract been cancelled now? (Answer) I heard it has been cancelled. The judge again (asked) Mai Yaoting, (Answer) I heard that a draft agreement has been signed for cancellation, according to newspaper reports. After the interrogation, the judge ordered that the trial continue at 1:00 PM on the 29th of this month and ordered Dou to accompany Sadeli to the court for questioning on the 29th or 30th. Then the court adjourned.

The Never-Ending Sheng Family Property Dispute

Li Sheng Yuju Accuses Yu You of Property Division

The Inheritance Is Harmful To Such An Extreme

The Sheng family of Wujin, residing in Shanghai, has a large number of descendants, but since Sheng Xingsun and his wife Zhuang successively passed away, the children of each branch have been engaged in repeated litigation over the inheritance of millions of dollars of ancestral property, which was unevenly distributed. Litigation has become even more intense since 1927. One case is not settled, and another arises, which can be described as the champion of litigation in Shanghai. To this day, there are still cases pending in the First Special District Court. Unexpectedly, lawsuits have been heard again. Sheng Xingsun had five sons, Kuichen, Aichen, Zechen, Panchen, and Pinchen, and four daughters. Aichen died in 1919 and had no children during his lifetime. Therefore, in 1915, Sheng Yuju, the daughter of Kuichen's eldest son, was married to the Li family of Hefei as a daughter-in-law. After Aichen died, the clan adopted Zechen's son Yu You to succeed him because he had no heirs. However, the property left by Sheng Xingsun at the time of his death, in addition to being divided by the sons, also included a minister's payment to establish the Yuzhai Charity Estate. In 1927, the National Revolutionary Army recovered Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and the capital was established in Nanjing. At that time, the trend of confiscating the property of corrupt local tyrants was very prevalent, and the descendants of the Sheng family took out 60% of the Charity Estate's property for equal distribution among the five sons and four daughters. Aichen's one-ninth share was inherited by his adopted son Yu You. Later, the property left by Sheng's wife Zhuang was divided, and Aichen's share of approximately 70,000 yuan was also inherited by Yu You. At that time, Wang Shengrong, the concubine daughter of Kuichen, had already married into the Wang family, and she was involved in litigation with Yu You. Rong claimed that she was Aichen's adopted daughter and should inherit Aichen's property. Although Yu You objected, the First Special Court had already ruled in favor of Wang Shengrong. Because it has not been completely determined, whether another wave can be launched is still unknown. Now, Li Sheng Yuju has again retained a lawyer to file a lawsuit against Yu You for property division. It is claimed that Sheng Yuju is in fact Aichen's adopted daughter. Aichen's share of (1) one-ninth of the Yuzhai Charity Estate's property and (2) 70,000 yuan of Lady Zhuang's inheritance should be divided into three shares, and Sheng Yuju should receive one-third. It is requested that Yu You hand over the property and divide it according to law, and Wang Shengrong is listed as the second defendant. Yesterday morning, Judge Luo Chongtai of the First Special Court opened a hearing. Neither the plaintiff nor the defendant appeared in person, and each was represented by their attorneys. The plaintiff's lawyer first stated the intent of the prosecution and then presented the gift list from the plaintiff's wedding, Sheng Xingsun's handwritten note, and the letter from his eldest grandson Sheng Yucheng as evidence, and requested that Yucheng and Sheng Linhuai, the brigade commander of the Sheng family, be summoned to court for questioning. The lawyers for the two defendants then made statements in turn. The defendant completely denied the plaintiff's claims. As for the two witnesses that the plaintiff requested to summon, the defendant also found it difficult to agree because Yucheng was the plaintiff's elder brother, and Linhuai had voluntarily testified in court in another case, but he requested benefits, which the defendant refused. Therefore, the defendant could not believe his testimony this time. Judge Luo ruled that the case still required investigation and adjourned the hearing to the 13th of this month.

Accusation of Adultery After Divorce

Tang Zhixiang Still Wants to Exercise Spousal Rights

Jiang Youqing Reserves the Right to Counterclaim for False Accusation

Tang Zhixiang, a 27-year-old Chongming native who works as a sock weaver at the Xinghua Sock Factory at 37, the intersection of Tokyo Road and Putuo Road in the western district of the Public Concession, married Huang Xiuying (23 years old this year), a woman from his hometown, two years ago in his hometown. After the marriage, he brought her to Shanghai, where they worked and lived in the same sock factory. Initially, their love was strong, but later, Tang wandered around and spent money extravagantly, abusing his wife, which led to a breakdown in their affection. On February 17th of the lunar calendar this spring, the couple voluntarily agreed to divorce, with the woman compensating the man 245 yuan. They drew up a written agreement, each holding a copy as proof, which stated that the man and woman could marry separately and would not interfere with each other. After Xiuying divorced Tang, she met Jiang Youqing, a 29-year-old from the same hometown and industry, who was not yet married. Through matchmaking, she married Jiang as his wife and married him on March 10th of the lunar calendar. The couple worked together in the Yuda Sock Factory at 19 Dongning Lane, Jiaxini Road, in the French Concession, and lived together in the factory's workshop. Recently, Tang Zhixiang, Xiuying's ex-husband, learned that Xiuying had been seduced into adultery by Jiang when they worked in the same factory and that she was now married and living with him. He couldn't help but feel jealous and burned with anger. He filed a petition with the Conciliation Office of the Second Special District Court, citing Article 1337 of the Civil Code, which states that men and women who have committed adultery cannot marry, requesting conciliation to prevent Jiang and Huang from living together and claiming that their marriage was invalid. After summoning both parties for a hearing, conciliation failed. Tang then filed a criminal petition with the Second Special Court, lodging a private prosecution under Article 256 of the Criminal Code, accusing Jiang Youqing and Huang Xiuying of consensual adultery and requesting an investigation. The court approved the petition. Yesterday, Judge Sun Pengxian summoned the defendants and their defense attorney Gong Yiren to court in Criminal Division Two. First, the plaintiff, Tang Zhixiang, said, "I married Huang Xiuying and came to Shanghai together to weave socks. She was seduced by Jiang Youqing, who worked in the same factory, and forced me to divorce. Because Xiuying married Jiang Youqing after divorcing me, I filed a lawsuit to prevent her. If she marries someone else, I will definitely not interfere." The two defendants denied having committed adultery in the past. The judge then explained to the plaintiff, "Your citation of Article 1337 of the Civil Code to prevent them from marrying is a civil matter and should be filed in the civil court, not in the criminal court. Now you are accusing them of Article 256 of the Criminal Code, which is seducing a married woman and is punishable by imprisonment for up to two years. Now that you are divorced from her, you have no spousal rights. She is an unmarried woman, and you have no right to control her." The defendant's lawyer then made a defense. The defendant also requested to reserve the right to counterclaim against the plaintiff for false accusation, etc. The court then declared the debate closed and scheduled the sentence for the morning of May 31st and adjourned the court. During the trial of this case, relatives and friends of both parties were present in court, numbering nearly a hundred people. After the interrogation, they all rushed out in a crowd.

Longmen Alumni Association Established Today

The junior high school of Shanghai Middle School on Shangwen Road, Xiaoximen, was originally the site of the Longmen Academy. Since the academy system was abolished, the Longmen Normal School was established on its site. For thirty years, the Longmen Normal School was reorganized into the Jiangsu Provincial Second Normal School, and then the Jiangsu Provincial Second Normal School was reorganized into the Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School Normal Department. Although personnel have changed several times, the spirit remains consistent. Recently, the alumni of the Longmen Second Normal School and the Normal Department of Shanghai Middle School initiated the organization of the Longmen Alumni Association. It has been approved for establishment by the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters and has been prepared. It has also been approved and filed by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education. The inaugural meeting will be held today (the 28th) at 2:00 PM in the junior high school of Shanghai Middle School on Shangwen Road. Party and government organs have sent personnel to guide and supervise, and Mr. Pan Gongzhan and Mr. Zheng Xigu have been invited to give speeches at the meeting. A film will be shown and a dinner will be held that evening to strengthen friendship. It is reported that the alumni and faculty of the former Longmen Normal School, Jiangsu Provincial Second Normal School, and Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School Normal Department number around 1,800. A grand occasion is expected at that time.

Forty-One Reactionaries

Escorted to Suzhou for Trial

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau successively cracked down on 41 reactionaries, including Wu Zhen, and transferred them to the District Court. Lou Ying, the Chief Prosecutor of the Procuratorate, submitted the cases one by one for separate investigation. It was found that in addition to committing the crime of obstructing official duties, the defendants were also suspected of reactionary activities such as endangering the Republic of China. Therefore, with the approval of the Jiangsu Higher Court Procuratorate, all bailiffs were dispatched on the afternoon of the previous day, and two inspectors from the Public Security Bureau led police officers to bring out the 41 defendants, including Wu Zhen, and escorted them on the Shanghai-Nanjing express train to Suzhou to be submitted to the Higher Court Procuratorate for detention pending trial.

Shenglong Steamer Sinks Fishing Boat

After the Hetae Company's He'an transport was sunk by a Norwegian merchant ship near the Guanghua Oil Depot in Gaoqiao, the sunken ship and cargo have been salvaged by the customs. Work began on the previous day and is still in progress. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, a small steamer accidentally touched the He'an sunken ship, causing a yellow croaker fishing boat to sink. The details of this situation are recorded as follows:

Accidental Collision with Sunken Ship

At around 12:00 AM yesterday morning, a small steamer named Shenglong was towing a yellow croaker fishing boat, intending to sail out of the Wusong estuary. It was heard that the yellow croakers inside the boat were goods from Qiu. When the Shenglong steamer was traveling near the Guanghua Oil Depot in Gaoqiao, it was late at night, and the helmsman was careless, causing him to mistakenly change direction. Its hull crashed into the already sunken He'an ship. In a hurry, the helmsman feared that he would cause a major disaster, so he quickly reversed the engine, causing the bow of the ship to hit the sunken ship and the stern to damage the fishing boat, resulting in a major disaster.

Fishing Boat Sinks

When the Shenglong reversed, it did so at excessive speed, and the bow of the ship struck a large hole in the bow of the yellow croaker fishing boat that was being towed at the stern. The damaged area was at the waterline, causing the fishing boat's bow cabin to immediately flood, and the entire boat sank into the Gaoqiao sand river in an instant. The cargo and the hull were completely lost.

Steamer Flees

After the fishing boat was hit and had an accident, the captain of the Shenglong steamer realized that he had caused a major disaster and wanted to evade responsibility. He took the opportunity to untie the tow rope and secretly sailed towards Wusong. It was not until yesterday afternoon that the customs water patrol discovered that the small steamer had collided with the fishing boat and learned that the steamer's hull had also been damaged. It is now hidden in Wusong for repairs. The water patrol has summoned the captain of the steamer to Shanghai to investigate the truth of the matter.

Health Bureau Efforts to Prevent Epidemics

Four More Injection Stations Established

And Preparing to Build Isolation Hospital

The Municipal Health Bureau's summer health work began on May 1st. Due to the inconsistent weather, the number of people suffering from colds and epidemics is increasing, so it has stepped up its work since the previous day and has established four more injection stations in Nanshi and Zhabei to make it easier for citizens to get vaccinated. The bureau is also preparing to build an isolation hospital to facilitate group injections. Any group or large number of citizens who need injections can notify the bureau by telegram, and the bureau will send doctors to inject them. As for the bureau's preparations for an isolation hospital, they are also in the planning stages.

Grains Industry

Notice to Grain Merchants to Improve Domestic Wheat

The Shanghai Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes Trade Association Wheat Group yesterday respectfully informed fellow traders and vendors in various producing areas that since China established itself as a nation based on agriculture, the abundance of its products has been renowned around the globe, and the country should be rich and the people strong, competing with Europe and the United States. However, farmers have been clinging to old ways, not seeking to improve, resulting in a decline in product quality and a decrease in production. In the past two years, the annual import of foreign rice has reached more than 10 million bags, and the huge loss is not to be mentioned. In recent years, the annual import of foreign wheat has also been around 10 million bags. Ignoring the great financial cost, it flows out steadily. This is because domestic wheat products are of inferior quality, and rural farmers and vendors fill them with mud and make them counterfeit in order to make petty profits, which eventually leads flour mills to shy away from them. On the other hand, foreign wheat products are of good quality and have no damp fluff or impurities, so it is no wonder that factories unanimously tend to use foreign wheat and discard domestic wheat. If this continues without any attempt to remedy the situation, flour mills will almost be unable to grind without foreign wheat, and Chinese people will not want to use anything but foreign wheat. The flowing water is endless, when can it be stopped? It can be seen that the livelihood of farmers and vendors will be destroyed, and all Chinese people cannot but be worried. The members of this group are engaged in miscellaneous grains and are in fear, so they dare not be self-effacing and plan for ways to rectify the situation. However, this matter is of great importance and depends on the wisdom and efforts of everyone. It is hoped that fellow traders in the country will catch up quickly and urge farmers and vendors in the producing areas to earnestly rectify the situation and no longer fill wheat products with water and mud, thereby demeaning themselves. They must fundamentally realize the need for thorough reform. Those who stubbornly cling to old habits should be sanctioned. In this way, there is hope for the improvement of domestic products, manufacturers will have no worries about discarding them, and the source of foreign wheat can be cut off without resorting to resistance. Maintaining domestic products and blocking loopholes will also be supported by the Chinese people.

Chinese Association Re-elects Executive and Supervisory Committee

The Shanghai Overseas Chinese Association is the most historical overseas Chinese organization in Shanghai. Since the founding of the association by the Prime Minister, it has been 22 years. The association's annual meeting last year resolved to hold the general election of overseas Chinese at home and abroad on July 1st. Now, according to the order of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission of the National Government, the election of members in Shanghai will be held in advance, and Mr. Luo Ciqi has been specially appointed as the election supervisor. Mr. Luo has already arrived in Shanghai and has agreed with the association's re-election committee to elect one-third first, and the remaining two-thirds will wait for the overseas elections. The election of members in Shanghai will be held at the association's auditorium at 1:00 PM on Monday, the 29th of this month.

The First Day of the Kun Opera Performance

The Kun Opera Preservation Society, on the evenings of the 27th, 28th, and 29th of this month, held a Kunqu opera performance at the Lake Society of the Chen Yingshi Memorial Hall on Beijing Road to raise funds for the Xian Dian Opera Troupe. They specially invited famous figures from the Jiangzhe opera circles to perform together. I entered the venue at seven o'clock yesterday and found it already quite crowded, which shows the appeal of the event. The first play was *The Chain Scheme: Small Banquet*, with Yu Zhenfei playing Lü Bu, Zhang Zhaochun playing Wang Yun, and He Jianmei playing Diao Chan. Yu and Zhang are veteran performers in the opera world, and Ms. He is said to be performing for the first time, but her deportment was graceful and her appearance beautiful. The ensemble of this play was well-matched, making it even more splendid. Next was *Sweeping the Flowers* by Xu Yuanlai and Ge Qifu. Mr. Xu played Lü Dongbin with a calm and composed demeanor, and he has clearly studied the pronunciation and enunciation of the words. It is said that his singing, recitation, and acting styles have all been corrected by Yu Zhenfei, truly a worthy student of a great teacher. Mr. Ge's He Gu was also quite fitting. Next was Wang Fumin's *Dream of Infatuation*. Mr. Wang's *zhengdan* role is one of the most talented in the current opera world. The *zhengdan* in Kunqu opera is equivalent to the *qingyi* in Erhuang opera, and one must possess both beautiful voice and appearance to play it well. Mr. Wang has just returned from Beiping and generously joined the performance to promote Kunqu opera, a feast for our eyes. Mr. Wang's singing and acting have reached perfection, so there is no need for me to add further praise. Next was *The Shepherd's Tale: Longing for Home*, with Xu Liecheng playing Su Wu. He is the son of the opera veteran, Mr. Shou Xun. His voice was loud and clear, and his acting was also well-regulated. The person playing Li Ling was the owner of Yun Song Hall; his name is unknown, but I felt that his deportment and singing had many commendable points. Next was Qin Tongli's *Borrowing Tea*, his attitude was elegant and his comedic timing pleasing. Liu Tingsun played Xu Jizu, looking every bit the young dandy. Paired with Zhang Zhaochun's nanny, it was even more lively. *Combing Hair and Kneeling at the Pond* featured Xu Muyan playing Lü Bu. Mr. Xu has studied Kunqu opera for decades and is known throughout the north and south of the country. Paired with Ye Xiaohong's Diao Chan, it was even more cohesive. De Tian Jushi's *Marrying Off a Younger Sister* had a vibrant demeanor and extraordinary presence. Qin Wangjie's Meier and Qin Tongli's Du Ping were also very well-matched. Next was *The Jade Hairpin: Asking about Illness and Stealing Poetry*, with Zhang Weiru and Xue Yujin both playing Pan Bizheng, both elegant and romantic, and touching to the heart. Qin Wangjie's Guan Zhou Chang had a clear and bright voice and was originally a capable performer. The final act was *The Palace of Eternal Life: Burying Jade*, with Yu Zhenfei as Emperor Tang Ming, Xu Deyi as Chen Yuanli, and Zhang Zhaochun as Gao Lishi, all concentrating and giving their best, a truly outstanding performance.

Conspiracy to Murder: Apprehended

Detectives from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, while inspecting pedestrians in the Shiliupu area yesterday morning, encountered Chen Baoxing from Shaoxing, who was passing by. The detectives found his behavior suspicious and searched him. They found a pistol and one hundred bullets on his person and took him back to the bureau. Under questioning, they learned that Chen intended to go to No. 12, Jianli Lane, Huayi Street, to murder Yan Yongxiao, the director of the Zhejiang Nan Dian Industry Shanghai Joint Office. He also confessed that the motive for this murder was instigated by six people from Shaoxing: Yao Azhang, Yang Dahua, Zhang Jinshan, Zhang Jinshui, and others, who promised to pay him 1,200 yuan as a reward. The gun and bullets were given to him by the two Zhangs, he said. After obtaining the confession, detectives led by team leaders Gao Wansheng and Sun Caifu, along with Chinese detectives Bu Zongting and others from the Old Zhabei and French Concession police stations, arrested the two Zhangs and Yao and Yang at No. 8 Yulin Lane, Suzhou Road, and Room 36 of the Zhonghe Hotel on Fuzhou Road. They were taken back to the police station for detention and escorted to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division this morning. The Public Security Bureau requested that the four suspects be transferred to them for interrogation. Chen was then brought to court, and his testimony was the same as in the Public Security Bureau. The four defendants all denied the charges. The police station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, argued that the Public Security Bureau already had substantial evidence proving that the four defendants were suspected of committing a crime, so the police station did not object to the transfer. Criminal Judge Feng Shide reviewed the confessions and ruled that Yao, Yang, and the two Zhangs should be handed over to the Public Security Bureau's representatives for investigation and trial.

Gatekeeper Policeman

Qijin Bao Commits Suicide in Resentment

Due to disagreement with the Shop Owner

Qi Duobao, a 37-year-old Shandong native who worked as a gatekeeper policeman for a Westerner at No. 360 Haig Road, had served diligently for several years. He had disagreements with the shop owner, Gu Yuanmeng, and had several verbal altercations. Recently, Gu suspected Qi of stealing clothes, but Qi suffered this injustice and had nowhere to turn. He was also deeply afraid that the matter would be known to his employer, which would affect his job and reputation. He was extremely worried and unhappy and eventually developed suicidal thoughts. The day before yesterday, he stabbed himself in the neck and chest with scissors in his bedroom, causing severe injuries. He fell to the ground and died from excessive blood loss. His colleague, Liu Qinghe, caught sight of him and tried to dissuade him, but it was too late. He reported to the Westerner, who in turn reported to the Jing'an Temple Police Station. When the detectives arrived, Qi had already died from his injuries. The body was taken to the Feilun Road Morgue for examination. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei of the First Special District Court arrived at the morgue to investigate. According to the complaint filed by the deceased's cousin, Hou Shaotang, the deceased's family was all in his hometown, so he dared not arrange for the coffin and burial. However, a few days ago, the deceased had come to his place to talk about the quarrel with Gu, and his words revealed resentment and unbearable feelings. At the time, I tried to dissuade him, and he went back immediately. I did not expect that he would suddenly commit suicide, he said. Mr. Guo reviewed the confession and ruled that the deceased, Qi Jinbao, had indeed committed suicide by stabbing himself with scissors. The body was handed over to the Pushan Cemetery for coffin and burial.

Vietnamese Policeman Assaults Vendor

Ningbo Association Sends Letter to French Consul-General Requesting Punishment

The New News Agency reports: The Ningbo Association stated yesterday that they received a report from a fellow townsman, Zhang Wang, stating that her son, Zhang Yu-gao, was selling water chestnuts on Caishe Street in the French Concession when he was violently assaulted and injured by Vietnamese policeman No. 198. His injuries were severe, and she requested redress. After receiving the report, the association immediately sent a letter to the French Concession police authorities, requesting that justice be upheld. The original letter is recorded below: "Respectfully, according to the statement made to our association by our fellow townsman, Zhang Wang, she was born unlucky, her husband died fifteen years ago, leaving behind a son, Yu-gao, who was born posthumously. Because the family has no land, they rely on the No. 164 permit obtained in the French Concession Caishe Street, where her son, Yu-gao, sells green vegetables and water chestnuts to make a living. Unfortunately, at around 8 a.m. on the 27th of this month, her son, Yu-gao, had water chestnuts which he had sold from Xiaodongmen and brought to the Caishe Street to sell, when Vietnamese policeman No. 198 came, stepped on the water chestnuts with his feet, accused him of selling without a permit, and without any explanation, kicked and punched him, relying on his barbarity and acting violently. Yu-gao was injured, fell to the ground, and vomited blood. Passersby, seeing this, felt indignant. The Vietnamese policeman then brandished his gun in a threatening manner and swaggered away. By the time his mother rushed over, Yu-gao was still bleeding. They went to the Dada Zimin Bell Police Station to file a complaint. Although the son was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, the injuries have not subsided, and recently he has been urinating blood. If something unfortunate happens, how will they live? He came to us and asked us to find a way to help. After investigation, we found that the vendor holds the No. 164 permit and operates a stall legally. The Vietnamese policeman No. 198 acted arbitrarily and violently, kicking and beating Zhang Yu-gao and injuring him. The tragedy on Xinqiao Street has just passed, and the bloodshed in Caishe Street has begun again. The lives of citizens are not guaranteed at all. In addition to sending Zhang Yu-gao to the Blue Cross Hospital for treatment, we hereby request that Your Consul General pay attention to the illegal behavior of the Vietnamese policemen under your command, impose appropriate punishment on No. 198, and provide compensation for the victim's damages, in order to seek justice. We hope that you will investigate and reply. Respectfully, to the French Concession Police Department's Consul-General."

Bandits Conspire to Rob Gold Bars in Hotel

Detectives Arrest Them After Receiving Information

One of the Old Bandits is Sixty Years Old

Sentenced Yesterday After Trial

Shang Wu, the Chinese Detective Chief of the Di Siwei Road Police Station, detectives Liu Decheng, and others, arrested three bandits from Taizhou, Chen Xibao; Xuzhou, Li Zhiliang; and Zhuang Fuchen, in Room 50 of the Anle Hotel at No. 321 North Zhejiang Road at 11 p.m. on the 18th of this month. They confiscated one blunderbuss and forty-six bullets and handed them over to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation and detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xie-fen of the Special Court continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tian-yin, stated that the case was being rescheduled. According to the defendant Chen Xibao, he had previously discussed with Li Baochuan, who is still at large, and Li Zhiliang in a tea house in Caishe Street in the French Concession, intending to rob 21 gold bars worth a considerable sum of money from the Qingfu Shenzhuang Transport Company at No. 7, Liugui Lane, North Zhejiang Road. The gold bars had recently been smuggled from Hankou to Shanghai and were tax-evaded goods. This information was provided by Li Baochuan, so they went to the hotel, opened a room, and Li Zhiliang brought the guns and bullets for use. It was agreed at the time to go to rob at 7 a.m. on the 19th, entering through the side door of the company. Therefore, the defendant secretly went to the company in advance to identify the location, so as not to make a mistake. During the robbery, Chen Xibao was responsible for guarding the hotel room. However, Li Zhiliang claimed that he had picked up the guns and bullets on Baoshan Road during the Shanghai war, wrapped them in paper, and hid them in a tomb. He brought them to the hotel that day in order to sell them to Li Baochuan. However, Zhuang Fuchen flatly denied any involvement in the case. He only admitted that he was involved in the case of robbing Xu Yutang of 3,200 yuan in paper money that he was carrying on Xinzha Road around 8 a.m. on October 18 of last year, and said that at that time, Chen Xibao lived in Hongkou, and Zhuang Fuchen went to invite him to go to rob together, but he refused. Afterwards, the leader, surnamed Wang, told Zhuang to bring him 20 yuan, because he knew that he had asked him not to reveal it, but Zhuang swallowed it, etc. The above situation was all confessed by Chen Xibao, so he added a charge. It was found that Li Zhiliang and Zhuang Fuchen were soldiers under Sun Chuanfang. Today, the injured parties have not arrived. The police station believes that Chen Xibao's confession is credible and should be punished according to law. As for the Mauser gun presented in the case, since it has the Public Security Bureau's mark, it should also be returned. Chen Xibao then confessed the previous situation (the defendant was already sixty years old and looked very pitiful). Afterwards, the police station's lawyer stated that the defendant had fully confessed and was not without cause for sympathy, requesting that he be dealt with leniently. Li and Zhuang, the two defendants, gave evasive confessions. After Judge Xiao reviewed the confessions, he sentenced Chen Xibao to eight months in prison, and Li Zhiliang and Zhuang Fuchen to one year and six months each. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined was allowed to be offset at a rate of two days for one day. The guns and bullets were stored in the warehouse, waiting to be sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for collection.

Page 12

More than Sixty Companies in the City

Dispute Over Capital Reduction in the Hat-Making Industry

Mediation by the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday Morning Was Unresolved

More than sixty hat factories in this city, including Dong Hua Sheng, Xu Yi Yuan, and Xu Wei Ji, reduced the wages stipulated in the labor-management contracts due to the impact of the current situation, ranging from 40% to 60% of the original wage, causing opposition from more than three hundred workers. The Hat Makers' Union has requested the Social Affairs Bureau to mediate, but the matter has not yet been resolved. The union believes that the straw hat season is coming to an end and that the delay will endanger the workers' livelihoods. Therefore, at 9:30 a.m. yesterday, it sent representatives Wang Yu-xiang, Zhou Zhi-qing, Zhao Ting-ting, and Ding Song-wan, along with more than forty other people, to the Social Affairs Bureau again to request a speedy mediation. Yan Pei of the Third Section received them. The bureau had scheduled a mediation session for 10 a.m., ordering the workers to attend at that time to make statements. At 10 a.m., Wang Yu-xiang and Zhao Ting-ting from the labor side and Le Rui-sheng and Xu Neng-yu from the management side arrived. Section member Tan Pei-yan of the Third Section chaired the meeting. After persuasion, the labor side agreed to reduce the discount from 10% to 8.5%, with a minimum of 80%. However, the management side could not agree, resulting in another fruitless outcome. The representative of the Social Affairs Bureau stated that the wage rates of the various factories were inconsistent and that a survey of the wage rates of the various factories must first be conducted to create an average standard. The meeting was rescheduled for 10 a.m. next Saturday, still at the bureau. During this period, both parties will try to reconcile outside the bureau.

Municipal Hospital to Start Construction Next Year

The Municipal Health Bureau, in view of the lack of a large-scale municipal hospital with complete facilities in the city, has decided to establish a municipal hospital in the downtown area to benefit the citizens. The land has already been designated in the downtown area, covering more than eighty mu. As for the hospital's facilities and building designs, they have also been completed by the bureau and submitted to Mayor Wu Tiecheng for approval. Funds will be allocated in the budget next year for construction. As for the establishment of a municipal hospital in Zhabei, it cannot be realized for the time being due to limited funding.

The Songhu Commercial Community Retains the Director of the Ship Donation Office

Jiang Nantong, Director of the Wusong Ship Donation Office of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Finance, has been in office for two years, rectifying tax donations on the one hand and caring for poor ship merchants on the other. He has won the sympathy of all industries and businesses in Songzhen. This time, upon hearing the news of his transfer, all of them were reluctant to let him go. Yesterday, more than forty businesses, including the Songzhen Rice Industry, Ground Goods Industry, Fish Industry, and Southern Goods Industry, jointly sealed and submitted a petition to Zhang Yuru, Director of the Wusong Branch of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, asking him to send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, which in turn would ask the Municipal Government and the Bureau of Finance to withdraw the order of transfer, so as to take both reason and sentiment into account, and to protect the happiness of the ship merchants.

Minutes of the Standing Committee of the Nantong Association

The Nantong Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association held its first standing committee meeting at the association's location in the Continental Department Store at 5 p.m. on May 25. The attendees were committee chairman Zhang Xiao-ruo, Ma Jun-shuo, Chang Ji, Xi Ren-fa, Tang Yuan-ji, and Cao Feng-biao. Ma Jun-shuo chaired the meeting, and Ge Fu-tian recorded the minutes. The meeting was held as scheduled. (1) The chairman reported on the resolutions of the second joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees. (2) Documents from the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau: the election of executive and supervisory committee members and the distribution of duties were approved for record-keeping. (3) Expanding the organization and recruiting members: It was resolved to follow the resolutions of the second joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees, and Zhang Xiao-ruo was appointed as the chief recruiter, Ma Jun-shuo as the chief of staff, Zhu He-gao and Zhang Zhen-xi as the deputy chiefs of staff, and Lu De-sheng, Xi Ren-fa, Li Yun-liang, Cao Feng-biao, and Tang Yuan-ji as the chief deputy chiefs of staff. Xu Qiu-yuan, Ma Bo-xian, Mao You-ren, Yan Chun-yang, and Xu Geng-qi were also invited to be honorary chief deputy chiefs. All members of the executive and supervisory committees are naturally captains, and enthusiastic fellow townsmen are welcome to volunteer to be captains. As soon as the printed materials for the recruitment are printed, they will be distributed, and the captains will begin recruiting. (4) Committee member Cao Feng-biao proposed that Mr. Ma Bo-xian, the honorary director of the association, was honored to be appointed as the director of the Nantong Nursing Home, which added to the glory of the association. The association should present a plaque as a memorial. It was resolved to submit the proposal to the executive and supervisory committees for approval. (5) Committee member Ge Fu-tian proposed that due to the hot summer, the association should set up tea buckets in various places. It was resolved to approve the proposal in principle and submit it to the executive and supervisory committees for handling. (6) The proposal to request donations from the association due to the Lusi mutiny had been resolved at the previous executive and supervisory committee meeting and handed over to the standing committee for deliberation. It was resolved that in addition to Zhang and Ma, the two chairmen, and Xi, a standing committee member, making voluntary donations, Xi and Ge, the two committee members, would also be responsible for soliciting donations from all the executive and supervisory committee members. The meeting adjourned after discussion.

Mosquito Repellent Incense that is Different from Others Summer has arrived, and mosquitoes have also come into being. They choose to bite the fat ones at night, which everyone finds painful. The only way to control them is to burn mosquito repellent incense. There are many kinds of mosquito repellent incense sold on the market, mostly twelve coils per box. However, the Invincible brand "Mosquito Repellent Incense" of the Family Industry Cooperative has fourteen coils per box, which is two more than others, and the price is cheaper. In addition, there is also the Invincible brand "Loose-Packed Mosquito Repellent Incense," which consists of two coils in a paper bag for retail stores to sell, making it convenient for customers to buy. The large-sized "Loose-Packed Mosquito Repellent Incense" has 40 coils per box, each coil can burn for 8 hours; the No. 2 has 52 coils per box, each coil can burn for 7 hours; the No. 3 has 64 coils per box, each coil can burn for 5 hours. It is said that the price is only 90 cents per box.

All firms, factories, and individuals can directly contact the bank to open an account, without the need for an introduction. Both Chinese and Western checks are available for use. The interest rate is fixed, and the procedures are simple and quick.

If there are those in other cities who wish to promote this soap, they can contact the company's distributor at No. 66 Sichuan Road in this city.

The movements are sturdy, the colors and styles are beautiful, the timing is accurate, and the prices are low, truly the leader among national clocks. Independent Review Anniversary Issue: The anniversary issue of "Independent Review," edited by Mr. Hu Shih and Mr. Ding Wenjiang, has now been published in Shanghai and is being exclusively sold and subscribed to by the Modern Bookstore on Fourth Road. It is said that the contents of this issue include "The First Anniversary of Independent Review" by Hu Shih, a commentary on Communism and advice to Chinese Communists by Ding Wenjiang, "The Intellectual Class and Politics" by Jiang Tingfu, "What I Saw in the Rural Areas of Ding County Regarding Church Affairs" by Hengzhe, "Attention Should Be Paid to the Fundamentals" by Xiong Shili, and "How Should China's Illness Be Cured?" by Tao Ming, etc. Each issue costs four dimes, with a full year's subscription including postage being $1.60, half a year being 90 cents, and overseas subscriptions including postage being $3.20 per year.

Modern Children: "Modern Children," published by the Modern Bookstore, promotes children's science and uses interesting stories, talks, and other forms to describe natural phenomena and scientific news, which is particularly novel. This issue features an article introducing the adventure of French explorer Gilner delving into an active volcano last month. The description is extremely systematic, interesting, and suitable for children's reading, making it the most novel children's publication in recent times. Each issue is only six cents, and a full year costs $1.40. Members who join the bookstore's "Children's Reading Club" will receive a free subscription for the entire year.

A Specialized Book on Studying Destiny: Philosopher Wei Qianli, residing in Daqing Lane on Nanjing Road in this city, is proficient in the Book of Changes and deeply versed in the study of destiny. To facilitate people's study of destiny, he has specially compiled a book titled "Selected Essentials on Destiny," entrusted to the Dazhong Bookstore on Fourth Road for distribution. This book details shortcuts to fortune-telling, analyzes difficult points in the study of destiny, and is based on facts everywhere, using correct arguments as theory. The included sections on introduction, proportions, discussions, textual research, and judgment are described in detail and compiled in a novel way. Even without a teacher, one can learn on their own. It is truly a compass for those aspiring to study this path.

The 43rd issue has now been published. You are welcome to read a sample copy. Each copy is only five cents. It is sold at newspaper stands in this city and bookstores in other cities.

醫藥界 (Medical Field)

Chongwen Society Provides Medical Care: The Chinese Chongwen Society, located in the Xilin Nunnery on Xilin Road, behind the Baiyun Temple on Fangxie Road outside the Old West Gate, has observed that there are many common people in the vicinity, and at this time of summer heat, they often suffer from diseases and have no means to seek medical attention. Therefore, they have specially invited internal medicine expert Dr. Hong Songjiong to provide free medical consultations at the society from 1:00 to 3:00 PM on afternoons, without charging any consultation fees, in order to help the poor. This can be said to be good news for those struggling with poverty and illness.

畫展 (Art Exhibition)

Zhou Lengwu's Fan Painting Exhibition: Zhou Lengwu, a famous painter from Wujiang, resides in Shanghai and uses painting to entertain his parents. His works of flowers and birds directly emulate Wen and Tang masters, and he is highly respected by the literati. Obtaining even a small piece of his work is cherished like a precious jewel. Mr. Zhou will be holding a public exhibition of over a hundred of his detailed landscape fan paintings at the New World Hotel on the third floor from today until the 29th for three days. It is believed that those with a penchant for such things will surely want to see them first.

The Tianqi Painting Exhibition Opens Today: Mr. Zhang Tianqi from Wuxi, Jiangsu, has been teaching at the Shanghai Fine Arts School for many years. In his spare time, he enjoys creating finger paintings. Over the years, he has accumulated a chest full of works, which he usually does not easily show to others. Due to the request of many colleagues to view his works, he will be publicly exhibiting over sixty pieces at the Shanghai Fine Arts School for the next two days. Those who have heard of and admired his work are coming in droves, and it is expected to be a grand occasion.

Shen Shiyong Offers Calligraphy and Painting on Fans: The young calligrapher and painter Shen Shiyong received an invitation by telegram from a friend in Hong Kong in March to write epitaphs, which took up a month of his time. Since then, he has finalized the notice. To broaden his connections in the art world, he is offering to write calligraphy and paint on twenty fan surfaces, charging only one dollar per surface for the ink. Applications will be closed when the quota is reached. The receiving points are at the Jiuda Gift Shop on Second Road and the Shanghai Silk and Cotton Factory in Xiangfen Lane.

電影 (Film)

Recent Developments at the Black and White Photography Society: Since the national crisis, the film scene has been desolate. Although there have been a few individual film exhibitions, there has been no grand group film exhibition since the first film exhibition of the Black and White Photography Society held at the Times Publishing House. Recently, the comrades of the Black and White Photography Society, while concerned about the national crisis, have not neglected the pursuit of artistic progress. Therefore, they are still working hard on the development of the society. It is said that since June, a regular dinner meeting has been held on the first Wednesday evening of each month, so that members can bring their works for mutual study, and to select dates for travel to nearby areas in order to collect materials. It has also been decided to hold the second film exhibition in October of this year, and the deadline for collecting works is the end of September this year. It is also learned that members Chen Chuanlin and Dr. Lu Shifu, at the urging of foreign friends, will be holding a joint photography exhibition at the China Youth Association on Sichuan Road starting on June 10th.

天氣報告 (Weather Report)

Yesterday's Meteorological Forecast from the Xujiahui Observatory at 4:30 PM stated: The Shandong coast is cloudy with localized rain. The wind is coming from the southeast to northeast. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with fog or thunderstorms. The wind is picking up and is nondirectional, due to a low pressure system moving northeast-east. The East Sea is cloudy with rain or heavy fog, and gentle cyclones. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 73.9 degrees and the lowest was 58.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 88.7 degrees and the lowest was 61.9 degrees.

Reader's Advisory

如何讀書的問題 (The Question of How to Read)

Letter from Mr. Wen of Yangzhou:

I have a matter to consult with you... I believe that the current world is shrouded in economic imbalance. Strong and weak nations alike are experiencing great unrest. International conflicts are becoming increasingly sharp. A second tragedy is bound to happen. This cause-and-effect relationship is worth exploring, and a reasonable future organization is even more worth studying. Domestically, however, the violent are breaking into homes, and politics remain dark. Partition and annexation are both possible. Moreover, the social economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, and starving people are ready to revolt. External troubles are indeed cause for concern, but internal turmoil is even more frightening. How can we achieve domestic peace, and how can we repel foreign aggression? This poses a serious problem.

Political and economic studies have always been my forte. However, during my university years, I lacked effective reading methods. Although I studied diligently for several years, my gains were quite superficial. Since entering the workforce, my busy schedule has further prevented me from continuing my exploration. My lack of academic knowledge is a constant source of distress. Worries about the times and the world have only increased my anxiety. Therefore, I have decided to study abroad during the summer to engage in a planned academic pursuit. I am unwilling to squander my hard-earned money, nor am I willing to waste my precious energy. I have drafted a reading plan to proceed step by step, grounded in reality, and to conduct thorough research. However, due to my limited knowledge, I am sure that my draft is full of errors. I specifically request that your column provide guidance, to serve as my compass. I am deeply grateful! The draft reading plan is attached below:

"Draft Reading Plan" - Three years of pre-study in Japan, divided into three stages: Stage 1: Language learning and review of basic knowledge. During this stage, in addition to focusing on language learning, I will select the most important classics and read them periodically according to the following categories: (1) Economics: Principles of Economics, World Economic History, History of Economic Thought, Economic Policy, Current Situation of the World and Chinese Economy. (2) Politics: Political Science and Constitution, World and Chinese Political History, History of Political Thought, International Public and Private Law, Current Status of Politics in Various Countries. (3) Society: Principles of Sociology, Social Trends, Major Social Problems in Various Countries. (4) Finance: Principles of Finance, Financial History of Various Countries, Current Status of Chinese Finance. (5) Principles and Applications of Statistics. Stage 2: Preliminary research: Focus on exploring the following issues: (1) Research on Economic Systems and Economic Organizations; (2) Research on Rural Economy and Rural Society; (3) Research on Land Systems and Tax Policies; (4) Research on World Population and Food Problems; (5) Research on International Economics and Weak Nations; (6) Research on Labor Problems and Factory Management; (7) Research on Municipal Problems and Local Autonomy. During this stage, I should engage in the following activities: (1) Sightseeing in various parts of Japan; (2) Reports on preliminary research; (3) Introduction and translation of famous works. Stage 3: Research on specialized problems: (1) Research Focus: A. Proper allocation of global food and population, and reasonable organization of international economy; B. Relief plans for urban expansion and rural decline; C. Design and implementation of Chinese land distribution and rural construction. (2) Reports on specialized research. During these three years in Japan, I will pay close attention to the following aspects: A. Japanese people and national character; B. Reasons for the success of the Meiji Restoration in Japan; C. Overview of Japanese politics, economy, and society; D. Reasonable solutions to Sino-Japanese problems. After completing the study in Japan, I will immediately engage in two major tasks: (1) Investigation: A. Travel to India, Soviet Russia, and Denmark. B. Observation and work in various rural areas in China. (2) Writing of specialized works.

Ministry Orders Changes to Elementary and Secondary School Graduation Joint Examinations

丨Elementary school joint examinations need not be held uniformly 丨Junior high schools can use sampling examination method

Hebei suspends elementary and secondary school joint examinations 丨Hunan Education Department's opinion on curriculum standards

For the past year, the Ministry of Education's promulgation of regulations for joint graduation examinations for elementary and secondary school students has been strictly implemented and tested in various provinces and cities. However, the results are difficult to ascertain. Now, as the summer vacation and the examination period approach, the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities have, based on actual difficulties, submitted requests to the Ministry of Education to change the elementary and secondary school graduation joint examinations and to revise the examination regulations. Such requests are becoming more frequent daily. The Ministry of Education, constrained by the regulations, finds it difficult to approve them. However, the actual difficulties in various provinces and cities cannot be completely dismissed. Therefore, it has taken into account the circumstances of various regions and made appropriate changes. For example, on the 26th, the Ministry of Education telegraphed the Hebei Education Department to temporarily postpone the current elementary and secondary school graduation joint examinations. On the 27th, it approved the Jiangsu Education Department's changes to the elementary school graduation joint examinations in various counties. In addition, the Ministry of Education has approved the Hunan Education Department Director Zhu Jingnong's request to allow sampling examinations for junior high school graduates and to stop holding graduation joint examinations for elementary schools, as well as two points regarding the request to revise the secondary school curriculum standards. The Ministry of Education's original order is recorded below: "Having noted the submission, the Education Department should consider the transportation conditions when conducting the junior high school student graduation joint examination, and divide the areas as much as possible to facilitate the examination. If there are still schools where transportation is obstructed and it is difficult for the students to participate after dividing the areas, then sampling examinations are tentatively allowed. However, detailed sampling examination methods should be strictly defined and submitted to the Ministry for approval before implementation to avoid abuse. Students who fail one or two subjects in the junior high school graduation joint examination shall not be eligible to apply for admission to higher education with graduation qualifications. Those who apply for admission with equivalent academic qualifications will be heard. Regarding the two opinions (attached) submitted regarding the revision of the curriculum, they have been copied and sent to the Curriculum Standards Compilation Committee for Elementary and Secondary Schools for review and to determine the examination subjects. The Ministry has clearly stipulated this in the Interim Regulations on Joint Graduation Examinations for Elementary and Secondary School Students, and it is not appropriate to reduce them. As for elementary school subjects, complete tests may be conducted, or one or two additional subjects may be tested in addition to the prescribed joint examination subjects. Graduation joint examinations for elementary school students should be handled separately as appropriate, but need not be abolished uniformly. The above points should be followed accordingly, and this order is given."

湘敎廳長請求修改中學課程標準之兩項意見 (Two Opinions from the Hunan Education Department Director Requesting Revision of the Secondary School Curriculum Standards)

(1) There should be differences in the subjects and content studied by male and female students: "The subjects prescribed for the joint examination, with the exception of English in junior high school, are all subjects stipulated as compulsory in the interim curriculum standards. There is no room for further discussion regarding the joint examination of students in compulsory subjects. However, judging from the results of the previous joint examination, there are significant differences in the achievements of male and female students. Although there are many reasons for this, the question of whether male and female students must study the same curriculum is a matter that urgently needs thorough investigation. According to the current curriculum standards, with the exception of military training and military nursing, the curriculum for all subjects is the same for both male and female students. In terms of intelligence, there is no absolute difference between the two sexes. However, in terms of gender characteristics and needs, it is impossible not to carefully consider whether the two sexes are completely the same. In addition, according to the Educational Objectives and Implementation Guidelines of the Republic of China, 'Women's education must also focus on cultivating sound moral character, maintaining the qualities of motherhood, and building good family and social life.' It follows that women's education should have its own unique qualities. If these qualities are to be cultivated, should there be differences from men in terms of curriculum subjects and content? This should be given attention."

(2) The inappropriateness of not dividing high school students into streams: "In the late Qing Dynasty and the early Republic of China, secondary schools had divisions for arts and sciences. When the new education system was implemented in 1923, high school general courses also had two groups, the first and second, to allow students to choose between arts and sciences. After the establishment of the University Council, the high school general course was no longer divided into groups. According to Article 1 of the Secondary School Law, secondary schools prepare students for higher education and employment. From the perspective of higher education, students who go on to higher education should have a considerable understanding of modern scientific knowledge as a foundation for studying advanced knowledge. However, students preparing to enter university arts and science faculties have different aspirations. Should the high school curriculum be adapted separately? From the perspective of employment, should the educational materials for each subject stipulated in the current curriculum standards be necessary for employment after graduation? This should be studied. Current high school students have submitted requests to the Education Department to restore the arts and sciences streaming system."

"The Education Department did not dare to dismiss this outright, so it is specifically submitted for review."

部院會商檢查電影事宜 (Ministries and Courts Discuss Film Inspection Matters)

The Secretariat of the Executive Yuan sent a letter to the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, requesting them to send representatives to discuss the inspection of films and the establishment of a Bureau of Educational Films. A meeting was held at the Executive Yuan at 9:00 AM on the 26th. Those present included Li Shengwu, Secretary of the Central Political Committee; Hu Mai, Secretary of the Executive Yuan; Li Songfeng, Director of the Police Affairs Department of the Ministry of Interior; Guo Youshou, Specialist of the Ministry of Education; and Zhang Jiong, Director of the Social Affairs Department. Two methods were agreed upon: (1) Before the central government decides on an overall method, matters concerning film inspection will be handled as before. (2) Regarding the statutory specialized agency established by the Central Standing Committee to handle film matters, the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education will separately discuss and decide on methods, submit them to the Executive Yuan for decision, and then submit them to the central government for adoption.

敎部　敎育年鑑陸續付印 (The Ministry of Education's Education Yearbook is Being Printed Successively)

The materials collected for the Chinese Education Yearbook, edited by the Ministry of Education, have been submitted by most provinces and cities, except for those from Guangdong, which have not arrived, and those from the border provinces and Liaoning, which have not been fully submitted. The total number of words in the yearbook is approximately 2.1 million to 2.5 million words. Approximately 70-80% of the drafts have been completed. The drafts from various departments and offices will be initially reviewed by each department and office, and then finally reviewed by specialists, directors, counselors, and the chief and deputy editors. It is scheduled to start on June 5th and will be delivered for typesetting and printing successively. The printing style will refer to the format of the Shen Bao Yearbook and the World Yearbook.

Recent News from the General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts

Difficult to Establish by June 1st

The General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts, since the Design Committee elected Gu Shusen and two others to draft the general regulations, recently completed the draft. However, Director Dai Jitao has not returned from the Northwest, making it difficult to review and announce them immediately. The association will be officially established after the general regulations are promulgated. Previous reports that the association would be established on June 1st are impossible to realize. The association will remain at the Lizi Society (not move, as previously reported) until the new headquarters is built. Currently, in China, except for Tibet, Qinghai, Gansu, and Xinjiang, most provinces and cities have established Boy Scout troops. Roughly, there are already eight hundred and some troops. Jiangsu Province has the most, with nearly two hundred troops. Provinces and cities that have established Boy Scout Provincial Councils (a provincial council can be established if a province has ten county councils) currently include Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and the cities of Beijing and Shanghai.

Zhejiang's Third Provincial Games Opened Yesterday

Competitions Proceeded as Usual in Torrential Rain

Whether Today's Events Can Be Held Depends on the Weather

Seven New Records Created

The third Zhejiang Provincial Games opened at 9:00 AM yesterday at the National Games Field in Meidong Gaoqiao, Hangzhou. The sky was overcast and drizzling. During the parade, a school of aviation unexpectedly sent airplanes to circle the air and scatter leaflets, which added to the atmosphere of the venue. However, the audience was not large. The opening speeches were very long. The speeches by the representatives of the Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government took a total of three-quarters of an hour. The number of participants in this competition was not large, but there were many groups, which reduced interest. The venue was neatly arranged, and the audience consisted mostly of children and women. All the prizes were displayed on the stage, a feast for the eyes. The perimeter of the field was guarded by male and female student volunteers, as well as soldiers and police, and the order was very good. At the opening in the morning, the sky was overcast and drizzling. By the afternoon, it cleared up and a little sunshine appeared, but it was fleeting. At 3:30 PM, just as the competition was becoming intense, dark clouds suddenly gathered, and torrential rain poured down. The audience scattered to take shelter, but the competition continued as usual. Umbrellas were useless, and the athletes and staff were all soaked to the bone. The rain became heavier and heavier, and the field was flooded. The competition had to be stopped. Whether the events can be held tomorrow depends on the weather.

Grand Opening

Guests Present: Lu Diping, the president of the games, was unable to return from Beijing due to official business and entrusted Chen Bulei to preside over everything. Those present on the day included vice presidents Lü Mihao and Chen Bulei, provincial party committee members Xu Shaodi, Hu Jianzhong, Luo Tian, and Fang Qingru, provincial government secretary-general Lu Dai, director of the Construction Department Zeng Yangfu, director of the Security Department Yu Jishi, director of the Central Aviation Office Ge Jingen, principal of the Aviation School Mao Bangchu, acting principal of Zhejiang University Wang Shiying, principal of the Senior High School Ye Suzhong, president of the High Court Zheng Wenli, chief prosecutor Zheng Tian, president of Hangzhou Normal School Zhang Yinian, director of the National Arts Hall Su Jingyou, and mayor of Hangzhou Zhao Zhiyou, totaling more than thirty people.

Opening of the Games: The opening was announced at 9:00 AM. First, the band played music, which was melodious and rhythmic. Then, all the staff and athletes paraded around the field. The organizing committee had previously requested the Aviation Academy to send a new-style Airplane No. 13 to fly high in the sky above the venue, scattering leaflets, circling back and forth, sometimes high and sometimes low, sometimes fast and sometimes slow. Thousands of colorful papers fluttered like butterflies. Next, everyone stood at attention, the music played, the flag was raised, and the party song was sung. After paying respects to the party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, Vice President Chen Bulei delivered the opening remarks on behalf of President Lu Diping.

Chairman's Speech: It was briefly mentioned that today the province is holding the third provincial games. President Lu, the chairman, is in Beijing on official business and has specially requested this seat to deliver a speech, briefly mentioning that the province's first provincial games were held in March of the 19th year, the second was held in September of the 20th year, and this is the third time. In the first half of last year, due to the current situation and various relationships, it was not possible to hold them. In the second half of last year, district games were held in accordance with the outline of the provincial sports games, divided into four districts: Hangzhou, Ningbo, Jinhua, and Wenzhou. Schools and the public participated. One aspect of this games is to review the progress of the province's sports achievements in recent years, and at the same time, to prepare for the National Games. The athletes participating today are very enthusiastic, and people from all walks of life have come to visit, which is very gratifying to us, and so on. Next, provincial party representative Hu Jianzhong and provincial government representative Zeng Yangfu delivered speeches one after another, all of which were encouraging words. Then, Vice President Chen Bulei delivered a speech, followed by a speech by Aviation Office Director Ge Jingen, and a photo was taken to mark the occasion.

Seven New Records

A total of seven new records were created at the Games. In the 100-meter dash for the university group, Chen Hanzhang of Aviation achieved 11.7 seconds, the original record being 12 seconds. In the 200-meter dash, Chen Jialin achieved 24 seconds for the university group. In the past Chen Hanzhang made a record with Jin Huaizhi with 24.3 seconds, Chen Hanzhang of the Aviation team, achieved 54.4 seconds, beating the original record of 58 seconds in the 400m dash. In the 16-pound shot put for men's senior, university, college, and public groups, all new records were set. The best result was Yuan He's 9.71 meters in the public group. The original record was 9.23 meters by Leng Peiji. In the 800 meters, Le Yiqin from the university group achieved 2 minutes 15.8 seconds, the original record being 2 minutes 16.6 seconds by Zeng Zifu.
